***штурмовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовать.html>штурмова́ть</a> (13082)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">stürmen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to attack, to storm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовать.html>штурмова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šturmovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to storm, to assault, to conquer, to attack</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>штурм</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šturm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовик.html>штурмови́к</a> (9477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовать.html>штурмова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šturmovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ík</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовик.html>штурмови́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šturmovík</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовик.html>штурмовика́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовик.html>штурмовики́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовик.html>штурмовико́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stormtrooper
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовик.html>штурмовики́</a></b>-коричневоруба́шечники</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šturmovikí</b>-koričnevorubášečniki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">brownshirt <b>stormtroopers</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> attack aircraft, ground-attack aircraft</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a pilot of such an aircraft</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> climber, mountaineer <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">participating in an ascent</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>штурм</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šturm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> assault
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовой.html>штурмова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:авиация.html>авиа́ция</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šturmovája</b> aviácija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>assault</b> aircraft; low-flying attack aircraft; attack aviation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовой.html>штурмова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:атака.html>ата́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šturmovája</b> atáka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">low-flying attack</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>assault</b> attack</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовой.html>штурмова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:группа.html>гру́ппа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šturmovája</b> grúppa</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>assault</b> group</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовой.html>штурмово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отряд.html>отря́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šturmovój</b> otrjád</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>assault</b> detachment</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штурмовой.html>штурмова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лестница.html>ле́стница</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šturmovája</b> léstnica</i> ― <span class="e-translation">scaling ladder</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>assault</b> ladder</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štúka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штучка.html>шту́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štúčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штучка.html>шту́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штучка.html>шту́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штучка.html>шту́чек</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štúka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (small) thing</li>
<li>doodah, doodad; widget</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штучный.html>шту́чный</a> (29299)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štúka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штучный.html>шту́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štúčnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)шту́чнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)шту́чней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>representing a single piece, not sold by weight <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. a garment</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>manufactured individually, one-of-a-kind, not mass-produced</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штык.html>штык</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štyk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штык.html>штыка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штык.html>штыки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штык.html>штыко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bayonet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примкнуть.html>примкну́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штык.html>штыки́</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Primknútʹ <b>štykí</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Fix <b>bayonets</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> foot soldier, infantryman <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">as a counting unit of military strength; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сабля.html>са́бля</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sáblja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šáška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отряд.html>отря́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штык.html>штыко́в</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятьдеся́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сабля.html>са́бель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otrjád v sto <b>štykóv</b> i pjatʹdesját sábelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a force of a hundred soldiers and fifty cavalrymen</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">schūbe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">giubba</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">جُبَّة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jubba</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">long garment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:джемпер.html>дже́мпер</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">džémper</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зипун.html>зипу́н</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zipún</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***шум.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шум</a> (1100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šumъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шум</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šum</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шу́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шу́мы</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шумы́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шу́мов</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шумо́в</a><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Professional usage.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>noise, radio static</li>
<li>sound, murmur</li>
<li>uproar, din, blare, clamour, hubbub</li>
<li>whirr</li>
<li>sensation, stir, bustle</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шуметь.html>шуме́ть</a> (2639)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šuměti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šumъ</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ěti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шуметь.html>шуме́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šumétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прошуме́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нашуметь.html>нашуме́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пошуметь.html>пошуме́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make a noise; to be noisy; to rustle (e.g. of leaves)</li>
<li>to kick up a row, to make a fuss</li></ol>

***шумиха.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шумиха.html>шуми́ха</a> (25391)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шум</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šum</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шумиха.html>шуми́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šumíxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шумиха.html>шуми́хи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шумиха.html>шуми́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шумиха.html>шуми́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>clamour/clamor, brouhaha, fuss, uproar, racket, ballyhoo, stir</li></ol>

***шут.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шут.html>шут</a> (9117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шут.html>шут</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šut</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шут.html>шута́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шут.html>шуты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шут.html>шуто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>jester, fool (person in a mediaeval royal court)</li>
<li>clown, buffoon</li></ol>

***шутить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шутить.html>шути́ть</a> (2211)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шутить.html>шути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пошутить.html>пошути́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to joke, to jest</li>
<li>to trifle, to play (with)</li>
<li>to make fun (of)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шутить.html>шути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шутка.html>шу́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šútka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шутка.html>шу́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шутка.html>шу́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шутка.html>шу́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>joke

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шут.html>шут</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šut</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шутовской.html>шутовско́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šutovskój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">шутовство́</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šutovstvó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li>n class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Ты вот, такой-сякой, ― она <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">шутливо</span> ущипнула его за щеку, ― ты ведь совершенно мной не интересуешься! </span></li>
</ul></li>



</ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шут.html>шут</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šut</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овско́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovskój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>fool's
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шутовской.html>шутовско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колпак.html>колпа́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">šutovskój kolpák</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fool's cap</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***шутя.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шутить.html>шутя́</a> (19458)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шутить.html>шутя́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šutjá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present imperfective adverbial participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шутить.html>шути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шутить.html>шутя́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šutjá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>in jest, for fun
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шутить.html>шутя́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>šutjá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">seriously, in earnest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>easily, lightly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шутить.html>шутя́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto móžno sdélatʹ <b>šutjá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">you could do it in your sleep</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шутить.html>шутя́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отделаться.html>отде́латься</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šutjá</b> otdélatʹsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get off lightly</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всерьез.html>всерьёз</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шутка.html>шу́тку</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шухер.html>шу́хер</a> (24712)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">זוכער</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zukher</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">searcher</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шухер.html>шу́хер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šúxer</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шухер.html>шу́хера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шухер.html>шу́херы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шухер.html>шу́херов</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> police raid, (house) search
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шухер.html>шу́хер</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пацан.html>пацаны́</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Šúxer</b>, pacaný!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Cheezit, boys!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> turmoil, confusion, noise</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mess</li></ol>
